<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wassen.html>wassen</a> (2154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wasschen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wascan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*waskaną</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wed-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:water.html>water</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
